<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:формация.html>форма́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">formácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:формация.html>форма́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:формация.html>форма́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:формация.html>форма́ций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> economics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> formation, structure
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">обще́ственно-экономи́ческая <b><a href = vnd.unilang:формация.html>форма́ция</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">obščéstvenno-ekonomíčeskaja <b>formácija</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">social and economic structure</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> formation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">девонская (<a href = vnd.unilang:меловой.html>мелова́я</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:пермский.html>пе́рмская</a>, третичная) <b><a href = vnd.unilang:формация.html>форма́ция</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">devonskaja (melovája, pérmskaja, tretičnaja) <b>formácija</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Devonian (Cretaceous, Permian, Tertiary) formation</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fórma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-енный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:форменный.html>фо́рменный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fórmennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> uniform
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:форменный.html>фо́рменная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:одежда.html>оде́жда</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>fórmennaja</b> odéžda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">uniform</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:форменный.html>фо́рменная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:фуражка.html>фура́жка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>fórmennaja</b> furážka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">uniform cap</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> regular, downright
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:форменный.html>фо́рменный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скандал.html>сканда́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>fórmennyj</b> skandál</i> ― <span class="e-translation">absolute scandal</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:форменный.html>фо́рменная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чушь.html>чушь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>fórmennaja</b> čušʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">downright nonsense</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:форменный.html>фо́рменный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:плут.html>плут</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>fórmennyj</b> plut</i> ― <span class="e-translation">regular scamp/cheat/knave</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:форменный.html>фо́рменный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурак.html>дура́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>fórmennyj</b> durák</i> ― <span class="e-translation">perfect fool</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***формирование.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:формирование.html>формирова́ние</a> (4355)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:формировать.html>формирова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">formirovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:формирование.html>формирова́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">formirovánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:формирование.html>формирова́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:формирование.html>формирова́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:формирование.html>формирова́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>formation, forming, generation, putting together</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unit, formation</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:фора.html>фо́р</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ми.html>ми</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ро<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 7a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-форм-</b>; интерфикс: <b>-ир-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-ова-ниj</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-е</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***формулировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:формулировать.html>формули́ровать</a> (22325)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:формулировать.html>формули́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">formulírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сформулировать.html>сформули́ровать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to formulate, to phrase, to word, to lay down (rules, demands, etc.)</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:фора.html>фо́р</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:му.html>му</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ро<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:форсировать.html>форси́ровать</a> (12517)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">forcieren</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:форсировать.html>форси́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">forsírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to force, to speed up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:форсировать.html>форси́ровать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:звук.html>звук</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>forsírovatʹ</b> zvuk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to force one's voice</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to force a crossing <i>(over a river)</i></li></ol>
